msg:This homestay was temporarily booked two days before my stay, because I decided to change my plan temporarily and live near the ancient city of Dali. The owner is very caring. He took the initiative to contact me two days before check-in, and told me that he could send a car to pick me up at the high-speed rail station, which immediately strengthened my confidence that I did not make the wrong choice. On the day of arrival, the pick-up driver waited at the station early, and immediately helped with the luggage. After getting on the bus, he introduced us to the overview of the ancient city and the scenic spots along the way, and told us that if we need any help during the journey, we can ask him at any time. The B&B is near the south gate of the ancient city, only 100 meters away. There is a bustling snack street outside, and the transportation and life are very convenient. Turning into a seven-to-eight-meter-long ramp, you will reach the lobby, which suddenly opens up, as if you are in a quiet outdoor Taoyuan. The B&B has a large enclosed yard with a simple style like a Japanese courtyard. The memorabilia of the B&B and the Mingren Wall are displayed on the side of the corridor. Faye Wong, Dou Wei and many other celebrities have stayed here. The room of the B&B is in a three-story building next to the courtyard. The room is elegantly and warmly furnished. There are free Pu'er tea and a full set of tea sets, a balcony with a view facing the courtyard, and a smart toilet for washing the butt in the bathroom. In short, it is full of comfort. Full. Up to the top floor, there is a garden-like terrace with flower beds and skyscapes for guests to take pictures. There is afternoon tea in the lobby every afternoon, providing coffee, refreshments and beverages, and you can also chat with the eldest and younger sisters of the store. The most commendable thing about this homestay is the service and intimacy. The owner, the elder sister from Hunan, is very kind and warm. There is also a little girl from Shenzhen who is also very kind and meticulous. The other waiters are also very nice and responsive. When I go to Dali in the future, I think I will definitely go to this one again, and I hope to see you in the future.
